<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `data_goods_weight` (
  `goods_no` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '商品货号',
  `real_value` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '实际重量，单位g',
  `calculate_value` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '测算重量，单位g',
  `category_value` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '品类重量，单位g',
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '新增时间',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '修改时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`goods_no`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_general_ci COMMENT='商品重量'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_abnormal_work` (
  `abnormal_id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '异常id',
  `work_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '工单id',
  `status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '异常工单处理状态：1:待处理；2:已经处理；',
  `unpacking_num` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '拆包数量',
  `handle_admin` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '处理人',
  `handle_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '处理时间',
  `handle_remark` varchar(250) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '处理备注',
  `create_admin` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建人',
  `create_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`abnormal_id`),
  KEY `handle_admin` (`handle_admin`),
  KEY `work_id` (`work_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=269 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='异常工单表'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_abnormal_work_info` (
  `abnormal_info_id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `dbid` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '打标id',
  `to_where` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '库区{1:正常区,2:库存区,3:退换区,4:售后区,5:次品区}',
  `abnormal_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '异常工单id',
  PRIMARY KEY (`abnormal_info_id`),
  KEY `dbid` (`dbid`),
  KEY `abnormal_id` (`abnormal_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=753 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='异常拆包工单详情表'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_activity_fee_refund` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键id',
  `activity_fee_refund_no` varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '活动退费单号',
  `supply_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '供应商id',
  `goods_num` smallint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '商品数量',
  `pay_amount` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '支付金额',
  `pay_tool` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '支付方式:{0:转账支付,1:上传回执,2:分账}',
  `pay_status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '支付状态:{1:待支付,2:支付中,3支付失败,4:已完成}',
  `pay_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '支付时间',
  `pay_admin` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '支付人',
  `pay_doc` varchar(250) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '支付凭证',
  `pay_account` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '收款人账号',
  `pay_contact` varchar(64) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '收款人姓名',
  `pay_bank` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '收款人开户行',
  `cnap` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '联行号',
  `receipt_info` text CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '回执信息',
  `cnsmr_seq_no` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '支付请求流水号(分账)',
  `pay_fail_remark` varchar(255) NOT NULL COMMENT '支付失败备注',
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uniq_activity_fee_refund_no` (`activity_fee_refund_no`),
  KEY `idx_supply_id` (`supply_id`),
  KEY `idx_created_at` (`created_at`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `idx_csn` (`cnsmr_seq_no`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=36 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='活动退费表'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_admin_bank` (
  `id` smallint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `bank` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '银行名称',
  `bank_account` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '银行账号',
  `admin_id` smallint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '管理员id',
  `create_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '更新时间',
  `account_name` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '付款账号名称',
  `fribkn` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '47504' COMMENT '联行号',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=5 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='账号绑定付款账号表'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_admin_bonus` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '自增 id',
  `bonus_id` int unsigned NOT NULL COMMENT '绩效id',
  `role` tinyint NOT NULL COMMENT '角色{1:买手,2:商运}',
  `admin_id` int NOT NULL COMMENT '用户id',
  `record_date` datetime NOT NULL COMMENT '绩效月份(只到月份)',
  `bonus` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL COMMENT '奖金(小数点2位)',
  `created_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `updated_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  `kpi_id` int NOT NULL COMMENT '指标ID',
  `status` tinyint DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '绩效状态{1:进行中,2:已结算}',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx_admin_id` (`admin_id`),
  KEY `idx_bonus_id` (`bonus_id`) COMMENT '绩效id索引'
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=14 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='绩效'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_admin_bonus_kpi` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '自增id',
  `kpi_id` int NOT NULL COMMENT '指标id',
  `name` varchar(255) NOT NULL COMMENT '指标名',
  `algorithm` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'kpi算法',
  `period` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '考核周期',
  `definition` text NOT NULL COMMENT 'kpi 定义',
  `created_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `updated_at` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=4 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_0900_ai_ci COMMENT='绩效指标'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_admin_menu` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '自增ID',
  `mca` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '菜单模型M/控制C/操作A',
  `label` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '菜单名称',
  `label_pinyin` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '菜单名称拼音',
  `show_menu` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '显示到菜单',
  `pid` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '上级菜单ID',
  `level` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '层级',
  `url` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '请求链接',
  `sort` smallint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1000' COMMENT '排序',
  `create_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `update_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `mca` (`mca`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=301 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='ERP后台管理菜单'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_admin_menu_copy` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '自增ID',
  `mca` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '菜单模型M/控制C/操作A',
  `label` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '菜单名称',
  `label_pinyin` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '菜单名称拼音',
  `show_menu` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '显示到菜单',
  `pid` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '上级菜单ID',
  `level` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '层级',
  `url` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '请求链接',
  `sort` smallint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1000' COMMENT '排序',
  `create_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `update_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `mca` (`mca`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=253 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='ERP后台管理菜单'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_admin_menu_tmp` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '自增ID',
  `mca` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '菜单模型M/控制C/操作A',
  `label` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '菜单名称',
  `label_pinyin` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '菜单名称拼音',
  `show_menu` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '显示到菜单',
  `pid` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '上级菜单ID',
  `level` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '层级',
  `url` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '请求链接',
  `sort` smallint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1000' COMMENT '排序',
  `create_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `update_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `label_pinyin_test` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT 'test',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `mca` (`mca`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=244 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='ERP后台管理菜单'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_admin_operation_log` (
  `log_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '自增主键',
  `log_type` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '日志记录类型',
  `log_key` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '日志键值索引',
  `action_admin` varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '操作人员',
  `action_type` varchar(30) NOT NULL COMMENT '操作类型',
  `action_result` varchar(30) NOT NULL COMMENT '操作结果',
  `action_desc` varchar(600) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '操作详细内容或备注',
  `action_ext` varchar(5000) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '操作记录扩展内容，长文本格式，可能会有很多种数据格式',
  `create_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '更新时间',
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`log_id`),
  KEY `idx_create_time` (`create_time`),
  KEY `idx_log_type_key` (`log_type`,`log_key`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=243625128 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='管理员操作日志'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_admin_setting` (
  `setid` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `key` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '键',
  `value` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '值',
  `type` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '类型 1系统配置',
  `sort` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '排序',
  `remark` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '备注',
  PRIMARY KEY (`setid`),
  UNIQUE KEY `key` (`key`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1635 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='系统配置表'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_admin_take_stock_info` (
  `admin_id` int NOT NULL COMMENT '管理员',
  `normal_box` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '常规容器id',
  `blp_box` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '不良品容器id',
  `parts_box` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '配件容器id',
  `nodata_box` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '无数据容器id',
  `stock_box` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '库存分离容器id',
  `package_no` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '包裹号(扫描包裹号打标时才有,切换包裹时清空)',
  `normal_box_pici_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '正在打标的常规容器批次',
  `blp_box_pici_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '正在打标的不良品容器批次',
  `parts_box_pici_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '正在打标的套装配件容器批次',
  `nodata_box_pici_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '正在打标的无数据容器批次',
  `stock_box_pici_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '正在打标的库存分离容器批次',
  `need_parts_box` tinyint NOT NULL COMMENT '需要绑定配件容器',
  `need_stock_box` tinyint NOT NULL COMMENT '需要绑定库存分离容器',
  `create_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '更新时间',
  `package_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '绑定的包裹类型{1:大货包裹(BG),2:备货包裹(BH),3:前置仓包裹(QZ),4:达人售后包裹}',
  `desk_no` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '工作台',
  PRIMARY KEY (`admin_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='管理员点货信息表'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_allot_bh_data` (
  `arid` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键',
  `goods_no` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '货号',
  `user_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '用户id',
  `stockouted` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否断货过',
  `add_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`arid`),
  KEY `goods_no` (`goods_no`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='配货优先级计算脚本临时表'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_allot_detail` (
  `adid` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键',
  `sirid` bigint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '(废弃)入库记录id',
  `order_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '订单id(order_id)',
  `rec_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '订单详情id(rec_id)',
  `create_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '更新时间',
  `status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '状态{0:无效,1:有效}',
  PRIMARY KEY (`adid`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `sir_id` (`sirid`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `create_time` (`create_time`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `rec_id` (`rec_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=13374093 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 ROW_FORMAT=DYNAMIC COMMENT='配货详情记录'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_allot_detail_rule` (
  `adid` int unsigned NOT NULL COMMENT 'allot_detail的主键',
  `one_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '99' COMMENT '第1层:{10:现货,20:非现货}',
  `two_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '99' COMMENT '第2层判断（数据组同步）:{1:100B,2:80B,3:50B,4:C端}，用户净值非0时:{1:100B高净值,2:80B高净值,3:50B高净值,4:B端低净值,5:其它}',
  `two_info_type` varchar(150) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '第2层明细按条件顺序（数据组同步）',
  `three_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '99' COMMENT '第3层:{10:排单很久&gt;7天,20:一般久3~7,30:不久&lt;3}',
  `four_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '99' COMMENT '第4层:{10:非常急,20:急,30:一般急,40:非加急}',
  `five_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '99' COMMENT '第5层按条件顺序判断（数据组同步）',
  `four_is_green` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '第4层是否绿色通道:{1:是,2:否}',
  `four_out_reorder` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '第4层上一次订单商品被断货然后重新下单（货号维度）:{1:是,2:否}',
  `four_change_allot` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '第4层订单商品被“改排单”（SKU维度）:{1:是,2:否}',
  `four_has_as_order` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '第4层售后换货工单的客需（SKU维度）:{1:是,2:否}',
  `four_reorder_30` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '第4层30天内对同一个货号商品进行复购（货号维度）:{1:是,2:否}',
  `four_sku_num` smallint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第4层sku数量',
  `pay_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '支付时间',
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  `user_net_worth` smallint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '用户净值:9999表示数据表中没有，10000表示数据表中为0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`adid`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='配货明细配货优先级'</pre>
</div>
<div class="pretty">
<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_allot_gz_label_user_from_data` (
  `user_id` int NOT NULL COMMENT '用户ID',
  `is_order` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否激活用户',
  `two_type` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层判断:{1:100B;2:80B;3:50B;4:C端}',
  `two_info_type` varchar(150) DEFAULT '' COMMENT '第2层明细按条件顺序',
  `five_type` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第5层按条件顺序判断',
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  `is_100_1` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层100B第1个条件有营业执照认证',
  `is_100_2` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层100B第2个条件近3月单月拿货额&gt;=5000',
  `is_100_3` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层100B第3个条件近3个月有2个月&gt;=2000',
  `is_100_4` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层100B第4个条件近3月同一订单单款拿货&gt;=2件且单价大于等于20且总次数&gt;=2且近3月累计大于3000',
  `is_100_5` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层100B第5个条件近一年拿货额&gt;=2万',
  `is_100_6` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层100B第6个条件【最近3天新客且首单&gt;=300且不低于2件】 或 【最近3天新客且认证方式为档口拿货单/发货快递记录截图/后台账号主页截图+后台上架商品截图/收入流水凭证截图/与收银台和认证码合照】',
  `is_100_7` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层100B第7个条件历史累计拿货额&gt;=20W',
  `is_80_1` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层80B第1个条件近3月单月拿货额3000-5000',
  `is_80_2` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层80B第2个条件近3个月有1个月&gt;=2000',
  `is_80_3` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层80B第3个条件近3月单款拿货&gt;=2件且单价大于等于20且总次数&gt;=2',
  `is_80_4` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层80B第4个条件近一年拿货额[1W-2W]',
  `is_80_5` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层80B第5个条件最近3天新客且店铺认证类型为“实体”',
  `is_80_6` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层80B第6个条件历史累计拿货额&gt;=5W',
  `is_50_1` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层50B第1个条件店主认证答题通过且身份自选为B类用户的',
  `is_50_2` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层50B第2个条件近3月单款拿货&gt;=2件且单价大于等于20',
  `is_50_3` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '第2层50B第3个条件历史累计拿货额&gt;=5W',
  `first_time` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00' COMMENT '用户首单时间',
  `user_net_worth` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '用户净值(数据来源：yishou_data.new_user_feature)',
  PRIMARY KEY (`user_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='系统配货新逻辑对应用户层级(同步于data库)'</pre>
</div>

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_asynchronous_task_log` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'ID',
  `task_key` varchar(200) NOT NULL COMMENT '任务key',

  `parameter` text COMMENT '传参，格式json',

  `res_remark` longtext COMMENT '执行结果记录',
  `task_start` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '开始执行时间',

  KEY `idx_unique_key` (`unique_key`)

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_broken_debts_record` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '坏账表id',
  `sdr_id` int unsigned NOT NULL COMMENT '呆账表id',
  `applicant_id` int unsigned NOT NULL COMMENT '申请人',

  `ck_auditor_id` int unsigned DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '仓库审核人',
  `cg_auditor_id` int unsigned DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '采购审核人',
  `application_time` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '申请时间',
  `cw_audit_time` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '财务审核时间',
  `ck_audit_time` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '仓库审核时间',
  `cg_audit_time` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '采购审核时间',
  `status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '审核状态{1:采购待审核,2:仓库待审核,3:财务待审核,4:采购驳回,5:仓库驳回,6:财务驳回,10:申请通过}',
  `remark` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci DEFAULT '' COMMENT '备注',
  `update_time` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '更新时间,同时作为最后审核时间，审核时才会更新',
  `reson_id` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '坏账申请原因（fmys_stagnant_debts_reson）表，数据从呆账表过来',
  `last_auditor_id` int DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '最后审核人',
  `source` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '转入来源:{0:历史,1:呆账,2:欠货}',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `sdr_id` (`sdr_id`),
  KEY `application_time` (`application_time`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `update_time` (`update_time`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=163741 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='坏账记录表'</pre>

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_cross_storehouse_order` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'ID',
  `cross_storehouse_no` varchar(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '调拨单号',
  `stock_storehouse_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '归属仓库 (调出仓)',
  `type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '调拨类型:{1:主动调拨,2:订单调拨}',
  `status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '调拨单状态:{1:新建,2:已生成拣货任务,3:已拣货,4:已校验,5:已出库,6:已完成,7:已删除 }',
  `transfer_storehouse_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '调入仓库',
  `transfer_goods_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '调拨商品类型:{1:常规商品-正常品, 2:常规商品-不良品, 3:前置仓-正常品, 4:前置仓-不良品}',
  `transfer_reason` varchar(200) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '调拨原因',
  `transport` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '运输方式',
  `transfer_num` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '总调拨数量',
  `picking_num` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '已拣货数量',
  `out_stock_num` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '出库数量',
  `on_way_num` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '在途数量',
  `in_stock_num` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '已入库数量',
  `abnormal_num` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '商品在“跨仓调拨在途商品”列表被标记异常的商品数量',
  `create_admin` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '创建人',
  `create_admin_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建人id',
  `submit_admin` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '提交人',
  `submit_admin_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '提交人id',
  `submit_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '提交调拨单时间',
  `out_stock_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '最后一个包裹出库时间',
  `finish_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '调拨单完成时间',
  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `idx_cross_storehouse_no` (`cross_storehouse_no`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `idx_submit_time` (`submit_time`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `idx_finish_time` (`finish_time`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `idx_create_admin_id` (`create_admin_id`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=440 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='调拨单'</pre>

  `dbid` bigint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '打标id',

  `create_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  `supply_id` int unsigned NOT NULL COMMENT '供应商ID',
  `stock_source` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '新入库类型{1:采购欠货,2:退换货欠货,3:售后欠货,4:售后拆包,5:调拨,6:现货调拨,7:核销,8:其他入库,9:生产盘盈,10:售后盘盈,11:旧前置仓,12:售后拆包错发核销,13:退换货其它入库,14:寄售库存,15:达人售后}',
  `sku` int unsigned NOT NULL COMMENT 'SKU编码',
  `status` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '商品异常状态{1:异常待处理,2:审核中}',
  `cause_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '异常原因ID',
  `responsibility_department_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '责任部门ID',
  `responsibility_personnel` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '责任人员',
  `edit_user_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '修改人员ID',
  `edit_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '修改时间',

  KEY `create_time` (`create_time`),

  `pay_bank` varchar(255) NOT NULL COMMENT '收款人开户行',
  `cnap` varchar(30) NOT NULL COMMENT '联行号',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uniq_pf_no` (`pf_no`),
  KEY `idx_supply_id` (`supply_id`),
  KEY `idx_created_at` (`created_at`),
  KEY `idx_payment_at` (`payment_at`),
  KEY `idx_woid` (`woid`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=149 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='商品赔付审核主表'</pre>

  `second_exception_num` mediumint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '二盘异常数量',
  `last_admin` smallint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '终盘人',
  `last_num` mediumint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '终盘数量',
  `last_exception_num` mediumint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '终盘异常数量',
  `now_exception_num` mediumint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '当前异常数量',
  `inventory_detail_status` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '状态:{1:已盘,2:未盘}',
  `is_exception` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否异常:{1:是,2,否}',
  `inventory_times` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '盘点次数:{1:初盘,2:二盘,9:终盘}',
  `is_chayi` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '最近两次盘点是否异常:{1:是,2:否}',
  `source` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '生成来源{1:在库,2:盘点生成}',
  `create_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '更新时间',
  `second_stock_num` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '二盘库存数量',
  `last_stock_num` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '终盘库存数量',
  `diff_price` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '差异价格',
  PRIMARY KEY (`inventory_detail_id`),
  KEY `inventory_id` (`inventory_id`),
  KEY `ss_id` (`ss_id`),
  KEY `sku` (`sku`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=226202 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='盘点详情'</pre>

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_inventory_dp` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'id',
  `inventory_dp_no` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '盘点单号',

  `created_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  `begin_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '开始时间',
  `end_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '结束时间',
  `inventory_status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '盘点状态:{1:待盘点,2:一盘进行中,3:一盘已完成,7:待终盘,8:终盘进行中,9:终盘已完成,10:盘点已结束,11:已作废}',

  KEY `idx_end_time` (`end_time`,`stock_storehouse_id`) USING BTREE

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_inventory_result` (
  `inventory_result_id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `inventory_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '盘点id',
  `dbid` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '打标id',
  `init_ss_id` mediumint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '初始仓位',
  `inventory_ss_id` mediumint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '盘点仓位',
  `source` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '来源:{1:盘点单生成,2:盘点异常生成}',
  `result` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '状态:{1:异常,2:正常,3:货位整合失败,4:货位整合成功}',
  `in_where` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '所在库区:{1:正常,2:现货,3:退换,4:售后,5:次品}',
  `change_wave_picking_no` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '改排波次',
  `create_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '更新时间',

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_order` (
  `order_id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `order_sn` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '订单编号',
  `user_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `pay_status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '支付状态 {0:未付款,1:已付款}',
  `allot_status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '(废弃)配货状态 {0:未配货,1:未配齐,2:已配齐,4:无货}',
  `consignee` varchar(60) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '收货人',
  `province` smallint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '省份',
  `city` smallint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '城市',
  `district` smallint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '地区',
  `address` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '详细地址',
  `mobile` varchar(60) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '作废',
  `order_amount` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '订单金额',
  `mobile_encrypt` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_bin NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '收货人手机加密字段',
  `shipping_fee` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '预付运费',
  `real_shipping_fee` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '实际运费',
  `pay_tool` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '支付工具{1:支付宝,2:微信,3:银联,4:微信小程序(平安),9:货到付款}',
  `balance_pay` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '余额支付金额',
  `pay_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '支付时间',
  `add_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '添加时间',
  `custom_note` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '用户备注',
  `pay_ls_id` varchar(80) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '流水ID',
  `shipping_fee_derate` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '运费减免',
  `is_alone` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否一手币订单{0:否,1:是}',
  `order_status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '订单状态 {0:待付款,1:待发货,2:待收货,3:关闭,4:完成,5:部分发货,21:银联付款信息处理中}',
  `other_pay` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '支付金额',
  PRIMARY KEY (`order_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `order_sn` (`order_sn`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`),
  KEY `pay_status` (`pay_status`),
  KEY `allot_status` (`allot_status`),
  KEY `mobile_encrypt` (`mobile_encrypt`),
  KEY `add_time` (`add_time`),
  KEY `pay_time` (`pay_time`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=889000913 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='用户订单表'</pre>

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_pa_cash_log` (
  `id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '自增id',
  `order_no` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '订单',
  `tran_net_seq_no` varchar(30) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '平安返回的单号',
  `type` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '类型:{1:提现,2:充值,3:分账入账,4:提现失败退反}',
  `money` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '涉及金额',
  `need_cash` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '剩余需提现金额',
  `status` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '状态:{1:成功,2:进行中,3:失败}',
  `remark` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '备注',
  `create_admin` smallint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '操作人',
  `bank_no` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '交易时的银行卡号',
  `sub_acct_no` varchar(50) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '交易时的子账号',
  `create_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_picking_task_rule` (
  `rule_id` int NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '规则id',
  `origin` tinyint NOT NULL COMMENT '仓库{1:广州,2:杭州}',
  `status` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '使用状态{1:正常,2:屏蔽}',
  `picking_carry_box_num` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '拣货任务携带容器数,只影响多件少波',
  `bjbb_min_goods_num` smallint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '多件少波波次商品最小数量,即为多件多波的最大值,多件多波最小值固定2',
  `bjbb_max_goods_num` smallint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '多件少波波次商品最大数量,最小值大于多件多波最大值. 大于多件少波的就是单波次拣货',
  `many_piece_max_goods_num` smallint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '拣货任务最大商品数,影响多件多波和多件少波',
  `max_wave_num` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '多件多波拣货任务波次,全级仓区之前生成必须达到该波次数量,全级之后可以小于该数量',
  `only_piece_max_goods_num` smallint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '单件汇总拣货任务商品数,只影响单件汇总拣货任务',
  `current_space_level` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '使用仓区级别',
  `use_all_space_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '开启全级仓区时间,只取时分,为0时不开启',

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_service_order` (
  `id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '工单id',
  `p_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '父级工单【有值为子级工单】',

  `refund_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '退款渠道{1:一手钱包,2:支付宝,3:微信,4:一手币}',
  `refund_monny` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '退款金额',

  `wechat` varchar(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '微信账号',
  `compensate_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '补偿方式{1:补钱,2:返券}',
  `coupon_type` varchar(512) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '返券ID',
  `user_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '下单的用户id',

  `back_shipping_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '商品寄回时间',

  `out_shipping_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '商品寄出时间',
  `handle_status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '售后处理状态:{0:等待处理,1:等候寄回,2:换货-等候寄出,3:补发-等候寄出,4:退款-等候审核,5:退款-等候付款,6:退款-退款驳回,7:已完成,8:已结束,9:拒签-等候寄回}',
  `service_desc` text NOT NULL COMMENT '客服备注',
  `record_desc` text NOT NULL COMMENT '登记备注',
  `out_desc` text NOT NULL COMMENT '寄出备注',
  `out_desc_user` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL COMMENT '填写寄出备注的用户id',

  `end_desc` text NOT NULL COMMENT '结束备注',
  `reject_reason` text NOT NULL COMMENT '驳回理由',
  `add_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '登记时间',
  `policy` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '政策类型{1:普通退换,2:大客户退货,3:特殊政策,4:vip运营退货,5:一手币,6:无理由退货}',
  `defect` varchar(100) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '缺陷位置 （1.领子,2.肩膀,3.腋下,4.袖管,5.袖口,6.口袋,7.前上,8.前中,9.下摆,10.后背,11.内里,12.整体,13.腰头,14.臀部,15.裤档,16.裤侧,17.裤腿,18.脚口）',
  `picture` varchar(512) NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '质量问题图片',
  `adopt_refund_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '通过退款时间',
  `last_opera_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '最后操作时间',
  `user_refund_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '关联极速VIP退货ID',
  `is_exception` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '是否异常，1-异常，2-非异常',
  `is_alone` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否一手币工单{0:否,1:是}',
  `back_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '拆包入库时间',
  `end_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '结束时间',
  `handle_user` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '跟进人',
  `record_desc_user` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '填写登记备注的用户id',
  `service_desc_user` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL COMMENT '填写客服备注的用户id',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `os_sn` (`os_sn`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `order_id` (`order_id`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `goods_id` (`goods_id`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `problem_type_id` (`problem_type_id`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `handle_type` (`handle_type`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `refund_type` (`refund_type`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `compensate_type` (`compensate_type`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `back_shipping_num` (`back_shipping_num`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `out_shipping_num` (`out_shipping_num`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `handle_status` (`handle_status`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `add_time` (`add_time`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `p_id` (`p_id`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `back_time` (`back_time`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `rec_id` (`rec_id`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `user_refund_id` (`user_refund_id`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `out_shipping_time` (`out_shipping_time`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `idx_end_time` (`end_time`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=10143713 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='售后处理/工单表'</pre>

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_supply_apply` (
  `sa_id` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '待合作供应商申请id',
  `supply_name` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '待合作供应商名称',
  `apply_imgs` text CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '申请图片',
  `mobile_phone` varchar(11) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '手机号码',
  `wechat_num` varchar(25) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '微信号',
  `supply_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '供应商id，没有创建供应商时为0',
  `status` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '0:已关闭 1:已建档待合作 2: 已合作档口 3:一审待审核 4:二审待审核 5:已驳回 6:已经作废 7:草稿 8:未提交审核',
  `is_apply` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否申请为合作档口',
  `market_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '市场id',
  `floor` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '楼层',
  `area_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '区域id',
  `city` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '所在城市{0:未知,1:广州,2:杭州,3:深圳}',
  `supplier_num` varchar(20) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '档口号',
  `submit_admin` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '送审人id',
  `submit_reason` varchar(255) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '提审原因',
  `submit_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '送审时间',
  `create_admin` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '建档人id',

  `is_delete` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否删除:{1:是,0:否}',
  PRIMARY KEY (`cooperation_id`),
  KEY `supply_id` (`supply_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=365 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='供应商申请入驻信息'</pre>

  `supply_level` varchar(10) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '供应商等级',
  `auto_time` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '自动时间',
  `is_old_supply` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '新老供应商{0:新供应商,1:老供应商}',
  `substandard_rate` double unsigned DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '次品率',
  `three_month_shipping_count` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '90天发货件数',
  `three_month_substandard_count` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '90天次品数',
  `sale_level` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '-1' COMMENT '销售等级,数据同步:{-1:无,0:l0,1:l1,2:l2,3:l3,4:l4,5:l5,6:l6}',
  `refund_service_fee_rate` float(5,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '-1.00' COMMENT '退货服务费比例,数据同步',
  `update_sale_level` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '-1' COMMENT '销售等级,手动修改:{-1:无,0:l0,1:l1,2:l2,3:l3,4:l4,5:l5,6:l6}',
  `update_refund_service_fee_rate` float(5,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '-1.00' COMMENT '退货服务费比例,手动修改',
  `service_fee_rate` float(5,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '-1.00' COMMENT '平台服务比例,数据同步',
  `update_service_fee_rate` float(5,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '-1.00' COMMENT '平台服务比例,手动修改',
  PRIMARY KEY (`supply_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='供应商标签信息-数据组同步-数据对接人：方秋顺'</pre>

  `supply_character` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '商家性质{0:常规合作商,1:买手小店,2:小店渠道商}',
  `is_deduct_repurchase` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '是否转抵扣并重采：1=是 0=否 ',
  `return_limit_ratio` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '100' COMMENT '退货限制比例',
  `day_new_limit` int unsigned DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '日上新限制，为空则不受限制(已弃用)',
  `month_new_limit` int unsigned DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '月上新限制，为空则不受限制',
  `week_new_limit` int unsigned DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '周上新上新限制，为空则不受限制',
  `cash_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '提现方式:{1:验证码,2:爆版密码,3:免密}',
  `is_show_best_choice` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '是否展示严选品牌{1:是,2:否}',
  `contract_type_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '合同模式id，系统配置中的原因id',
  `is_push_wcg_plan` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '是否推送采购计划给第三方:{1:是;2;否:}',
  `is_sync_supply_stock` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '是否同步第三方实时库存:{1:是;2:否;}',
  `platform_begin_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '平台佣金协议开始时间',
  `platform_switch` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '平台佣金扣取是否开启{1:是;2:否}',
  `goods_exempt_examine` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '商品是否免除审核{0:否,1:是}',
  `supply_member_level` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '商家会员等级{0:未知;1:青铜;2:白银;3:黄金;4:铂金;5:钻石;6:王者;}',

  `updated_at` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  `stagnant_status` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '呆账状态{1:支持转入,2:禁止转入}',

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_wave_picking` (

  `update_time` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '更新时间',

  `full_allot` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '2' COMMENT '配齐情况{1:配齐,2:未配齐,3:今日配齐}',

  `bill_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '记录抵扣的哪个先货后款账单',
  `price` decimal(10,2) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '本次折扣的金额',
  `create_admin` mediumint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建管理员',
  `status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '明细状态{0:有效,10:撤销抵扣,失效}',
  `ded_type` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '(废弃)抵扣类型{0:采购抵扣,1:补入调整,2:补出调整}',
  `create_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `wdid` (`wdid`),
  KEY `woid` (`woid`),
  KEY `status` (`status`),
  KEY `bill_id` (`bill_id`),
  KEY `create_time` (`create_time`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=3128 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='抵扣明细表'</pre>

<pre>CREATE TABLE `fmys_wcg_plan` (
  `planid` int unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '自增ID',

  `is_share` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否分享{0:未分享,1:已分享}',
  `status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '计划状态{0:已生效,11:待审核(原计划草稿),12:作废计划}',
  `ptype` tinyint NOT NULL DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '计划类型：{1:系统计划,2:手动计划,3:多开,4:备货计划1(均码商品),5:备货计划2(非均码商品),6:重新采购,7:售后,8:时刻计划,9:爆款备货计划,10:买版计划,11:提前采购,12:提前预测计划,13:虚拟现货采购}',
  `remarks` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '备注',
  `check_status` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '(废弃)审核状态',
  `check_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '审核时间',
  `check_user_id` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '审核人',
  `check_remarks` varchar(100) CHARACTER SET utf8 COLLATE utf8_general_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT '' COMMENT '审核备注',
  `plan_type` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '计划类型{0:备货采购,1:损耗补采,10:客户线下需求采购,11:样板采购,12:厂源直采,13:邀约配货,14:当天备货}',
  `create_admin` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '关联管理员ID',
  `expect_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '预期采购时间',
  `done_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '完成时间',
  `plan_total` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '(废弃)采购总价',
  `plan_num` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '(废弃)采购总数',
  `special_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '专场id,走播秒发才有用',
  `stocking_id` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '爆款备货id',
  `create_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` int unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '更新时间',
  `is_dispense` tinyint unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否小店分发{0:否,1:是}',
  PRIMARY KEY (`planid`),
  KEY `pgid` (`pgid`),
  KEY `create_time` (`create_time`),
  KEY `status` (`status`),
  KEY `done_time` (`done_time`),
  KEY `idx_sid_ut` (`supply_id`,`update_time`) USING BTREE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=977678 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb3 COMMENT='待采购计划'</pre>

<script type="text/javascript">
    (function(){
        var tab_tit  = document.getElementById('think_page_trace_tab_tit').getElementsByTagName('span');
        var tab_cont = document.getElementById('think_page_trace_tab_cont').getElementsByTagName('div');
        var open     = document.getElementById('think_page_trace_open');
        var close    = document.getElementById('think_page_trace_close').children[0];
        var trace    = document.getElementById('think_page_trace_tab');
        var cookie   = document.cookie.match(/thinkphp_show_page_trace=(\d\|\d)/);
        var history  = (cookie && typeof cookie[1] != 'undefined' && cookie[1].split('|')) || [0,0];
        open.onclick = function(){
            trace.style.display = 'block';
            this.style.display = 'none';
            close.parentNode.style.display = 'block';
            history[0] = 1;
            document.cookie = 'thinkphp_show_page_trace='+history.join('|')
        }
        close.onclick = function(){
            trace.style.display = 'none';
            this.parentNode.style.display = 'none';
            open.style.display = 'block';
            history[0] = 0;
            document.cookie = 'thinkphp_show_page_trace='+history.join('|')
        }
        for(var i = 0; i < tab_tit.length; i++){
            tab_tit[i].onclick = (function(i){
                return function(){
                    for(var j = 0; j < tab_cont.length; j++){
                        tab_cont[j].style.display = 'none';
                        tab_tit[j].style.color = '#999';
                    }
                    tab_cont[i].style.display = 'block';
                    tab_tit[i].style.color = '#000';
                    history[1] = i;
                    document.cookie = 'thinkphp_show_page_trace='+history.join('|')
                }
            })(i)
        }
        parseInt(history[0]) && open.click();
        tab_tit[history[1]].click();
    })();
</script>
</body>
<script>
// 意图美化sql语句🤣
window.onload = _=> {
    let doms = document.getElementsByClassName('pretty');
    // console.log(doms);
    Array.from(doms).forEach (v=>{
        // 把 `` 反引号和里面的内容替换成黑色的
        let html = v.innerHTML;
        console.log(html);
        // 数字是绿色的
        html = html.replace(/(\=|\()(\d+)/g, '$1<span class="green">$2</span>');
        console.log(html);

        // 把单引号及内容替换成红色的, 
        html = html.replace(/'(.*?)'/g, '<span class="red">\'$1\'</span>');

        // 把()替换成黑色的
        html = html.replace(/(\(|\))/g, '<span class="black">$1</span>');

        html = html.replace(/`(\w+)`/g, '<span class="black">`$1`</span>');

        // 固定黑色的
        html = html.replace('AUTO_INCREMENT=', '<span class="black">AUTO_INCREMENT=</span>');

        html = html.replace(/ENGINE=(\w+)/g, 'ENGINE<span class="black">=</span>$1');
        html = html.replace(/CHARSET=(\w+)/g, '<span class="black">CHARSET=$1</span>');
        v.innerHTML = html;

    });
}
</script>
</html>
